src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Christopher_Nolan_TCL.jpg/220px-Christopher_Nolan_TCL.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Christopher_Nolan_TCL.jpg/330px-Christopher_Nolan_TCL.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Christopher_Nolan_TCL.jpg/440px-Christopher_Nolan_TCL.jpg 2x" data-file-width="6000" data-file-height="4000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Christopher_Nolan_TCL.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Nolan\'s hand and shoeprints in front of the <a href="/wiki/Grauman%27s_Chinese_Theatre" title="Grauman&#39;s Chinese Theatre">Grauman\'s Chinese Theatre</a> in Hollywood</div></div></div>\n<p>Nolan screened <i>Following</i> at the 1999 <a href="/wiki/Slamdance_Film_Festival" title="Slamdance Film Festival">Slamdance Film Festival</a>, and won the Black &amp; White Award. In 2014 he received the first-ever Founder\'s Award from the Festival. "Throughout his incredible successes, Christopher Nolan has stood firmly behind the Slamdance filmmaking community. We are honored to present him with Slamdance\'s inaugural Founder\'s Award", said Slamdance president and co-founder <a href="/wiki/Peter_Baxter_(filmmaker)" title="Peter Baxter (filmmaker)">Peter Baxter</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-325" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-325">&#91;325&#93;</a></sup> At the 2001 <a href="/wiki/Sundance_Film_Festival" title="Sundance Film Festival">Sundance Film Festival</a>, Nolan and his brother Jonathan won the <a href="/wiki/Waldo_Salt#The_Waldo_Salt_Screenwriting_Award" title="Waldo Salt">Waldo Salt Screenwriting Award</a> for <i>Memento</i>, and in 2003 Nolan received the Sonny Bono Visionary Award from the <a href="/wiki/Palm_Springs_International_Film_Festival" title="Palm Springs International Film Festival">Palm Springs International Film Festival</a>. Festival executive director Mitch Levine said, "Nolan had in his brief time as a feature film director, redefined and advanced the very language of cinema".<sup id="cite_ref-326" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-326">&#91;326&#93;</a></sup> He was named an <a href="/wiki/Honorary_Fellow" class="mw-redirect" title="Honorary Fellow">Honorary Fellow</a> of UCL in 2006, and received an <a href="/wiki/Honorary_degree" title="Honorary degree">honorary doctorate</a> in literature (DLit) in 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-327" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-327">&#91;327&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-328" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-328">&#91;328&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2009, the director received the Board of the Governors Award from the <a href="/wiki/American_Society_of_Cinematographers" title="American Society of Cinematographers">American Society of Cinematographers</a>. ASC president <a href="/wiki/Daryn_Okada" title="Daryn Okada">Daryn Okada</a> said, "Chris Nolan is infused with talent with which he masterfully uses to collaboratively create memorable motion pictures<span class="nowrap">&#160;</span>... his quest for superlative images to tell stories has earned the admiration of our members."<sup id="cite_ref-329" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-329">&#91;329&#93;</a></sup> In 2011 Nolan received the Britannia Award for Artistic Excellence in Directing from the <a href="/wiki/British_Academy_of_Film_and_Television_Arts" title="British Academy of Film and Television Arts">British Academy of Film and Television Arts</a><sup id="cite_ref-330" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-330">&#91;330&#93;</a></sup> and the ACE Golden Eddie Filmmaker of the Year Award from <a href="/wiki/American_Cinema_Editors" title="American Cinema Editors">American Cinema Editors</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-331" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-331">&#91;331&#93;</a></sup> That year he also received the Modern Master Award, the highest honor presented by the <a href="/wiki/Santa_Barbara_International_Film_Festival" title="Santa Barbara International Film Festival">Santa Barbara International Film Festival</a>. The executive director of the festival Roger Durling stated: "Every one of Nolan\'s films has set a new standard for the film community, with <i>Inception</i> being the latest example."<sup id="cite_ref-332" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-332">&#91;332&#93;</a></sup> In addition, Nolan was the recipient of the inaugural VES Visionary Award from the <a href="/wiki/Visual_Effects_Society" title="Visual Effects Society">Visual Effects Society</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-333" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-333">&#91;333&#93;</a></sup> In July 2012 he became the youngest director to be honored with a hand-and-footprint ceremony at <a href="/wiki/Grauman%27s_Chinese_Theatre" title="Grauman&#39;s Chinese Theatre">Grauman\'s Chinese Theatre</a> in Los Angeles.<sup id="cite_ref-334" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-334">&#91;334&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Art_Directors_Guild" title="Art Directors Guild">The Art Directors Guild</a> (ADG) selected Nolan as the recipient of its Cinematic Imagery Award in 2015, an honor given to those whose body of work has "richly enhanced the visual aspects of the movie-going experience".<sup id="cite_ref-335" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-335">&#91;335&#93;</a></sup> He was selected as the 2015 Class Day speaker at <a href="/wiki/Princeton_University" title="Princeton University">Princeton University</a>. "Nolan, more than a film producer, is a thinker and visionary in our age and we are thrilled to have him deliver the keynote address," said Class Day co-chair Hanna Kim.<sup id="cite_ref-336" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-336">&#91;336&#93;</a></sup> Nolan was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Empire_Inspiration_Award" title="Empire Inspiration Award">Empire Inspiration Award</a> at the <a href="/wiki/20th_Empire_Awards" title="20th Empire Awards">20th Empire Awards</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-337" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-337">&#91;337&#93;</a></sup> The director was also honored with a retrospective at the <a href="/wiki/Walker_Art_Center" title="Walker Art Center">Walker Art Center</a> in Minneapolis.<sup id="cite_ref-338" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-338">&#91;338&#93;</a></sup> On 3<span class="nowrap">&#160;</span>May 2017, Nolan received the 2017 <a href="/wiki/International_Federation_of_Film_Archives" title="International Federation of Film Archives">FIAF</a> Award before a special 70<span class="nowrap">&#160;</span>mm screening of <i>Interstellar</i> at the <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Goldwyn_Theater" title="Samuel Goldwyn Theater">Samuel Goldwyn Theater</a> in Beverly Hills.<sup id="cite_ref-339" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-339">&#91;339&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, Nolan was awarded the inaugural Vanguard Award from The Digital Entertainment Group, in recognition of his use of technology "to deliver increased scale and resolution, enhanced color and immersive audio to film audiences both in cinemas and in the home theater environment."<sup id="cite_ref-340" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-340">&#91;340&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Filmography">Filmography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Christopher_Nolan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Filmography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Nolan_filmography" title="Christopher Nolan filmography">Christopher Nolan filmography</a></div>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Directed_features">Directed features</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Christopher_Nolan&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Directed features">edit</a><span href="/wiki/BBC%27s_100_Greatest_Films_of_the_21st_Century" title="BBC&#39;s 100 Greatest Films of the 21st Century">BBC\'s 100 Greatest Films of the 21st Century</a> list.<sup id="cite_ref-346" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-346">&#91;346&#93;</a></sup> In the following year, five of his (then nine) films featured in <i><a href="/wiki/Empire_(film_magazine)" title="Empire (film magazine)">Empire</a></i> magazine\'s poll of <a href="/wiki/Empire_(film_magazine)#The_100_Greatest_Movies" title="Empire (film magazine)">The 100 Greatest Movies</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-347" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-347">&#91;347&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span
